  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c27cdd02-7ff4-4bc1-9ff3-b1a8c443aa4a'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

A bad s</span>
  <span id="freeText13917425277130799763" style="display:none"><i>Hailed as a major new talent in paranormal romance, Nalini Singh takes us deeper into the world of the Psy and the changelings in her latest extraordinary novel, where a gifted woman sees passion in her future - a passion that is absolutely forbidden by her kind...</i><br /><br />Used to cold silence, Faith NightStar is suddenly being tormented by dark visions of blood and murder. A bad sign for anyone, but worse for Faith, an F-Psy with the highly sought after ability to predict the future. Then the visions show her something even more dangerous - aching need...exquisite pleasure. But so powerful is her sight, so fragile the state of her mind, that the very emotions she yearns to embrace could be the end of her.<br /><br />Changeling Vaughn D'Angelo can take the form of either man or jaguar, but it is his animal side that is overwhelmingly drawn to Faith. The jaguar's instinct is to claim this woman it finds so utterly fascinating and the man has no argument. But while Vaughn craves sensation and hungers to pleasure Faith in every way, desire is a danger that could snap the last threads of her sanity. And there are Psy who need Faith's sight for their own purposes. They must keep her silenced - and keep her from Vaughn.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13917425277130799763" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div id="review_2414074222" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2414074222" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2414074222?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=superpowers-specialpowers">superpowers-specialpowers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2414074222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13075892901177098221"><b>Faith Nightstar (Psy) and Vaughn D'Angelo (Changeling)</b><br/><br/>Faith is the best F-Psy i.e. of the foreseers. She has been working since she was three years old and she could talk. She almost never leaves her home, she has security 24 hours per day, her meals are planned and if she has to make contact with the Psy who is responsible for her in certain intervals of time. Otherwise everyone is worried. Sometimes she is so lost in her visions of the future that she forgets to eat or drink.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>Faith had never</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText13075892901177098221" style="display:none"><b>Faith Nightstar (Psy) and Vaughn D'Angelo (Changeling)</b><br /><br />Faith is the best F-Psy i.e. of the foreseers. She has been working since she was three years old and she could talk. She almost never leaves her home, she has security 24 hours per day, her meals are planned and if she has to make contact with the Psy who is responsible for her in certain intervals of time. Otherwise everyone is worried. Sometimes she is so lost in her visions of the future that she forgets to eat or drink.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Faith had never left the compound on her own. They'd put her inside twenty-one years ago, telling her that her mind couldn't survive in the outside world, that the visions would come too thick and fast if she lived closely with others. She'd had no reason to disbelieve them and over the years, her home had become her chosen prison, a place she rarely left.</b>
</i><br /><br />Faith lives in a bubble. But lately she feels that she is going insane. Lately she does not think of the forecasting of business trends. On the contrary, she keeps dreaming of blood, murders and horrific acts.<br /><br />For that reason, she has decided that she needs help from an outsider and more particularly from Sascha, the Psy who left the Net and mated the Alpha of the DarkRiver pack.<br /><br />Vaughn is the jaguar and the sentinel of the DarkRiver pack. His Alpha, Lucas, totally trusts him -although Vaughn is more animal than man. When he was a kid, he had to stay in his animal form for a long time in order to survive and for that reason he feels more comfortable being a jaguar.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Are you sure I'm that logical?”<br />"No. But you're not an animal either.”<br />He leaned in close until he had her boxed against the wall, his arms on either side of her body. One simple lift and he could have her at his sexual mercy. 'That's where you're wrong, baby." He brushed his lips over her ear. "I'm as animal as they come." Before she could say anything, he pushed off and walked into the kitchen.<br />He heard the ragged gasp of her breath a few seconds later. "Are you really?”<br />He looked over his shoulder. "What do you think?”</i>
</b><br /><br />When hot-blooded Vaughn meets emotionless Faith, he realises that Faith is important to him and that Faith cannot be that cold and distant. He needs to connect with her, but her isolated life only allows him to make baby steps to win her heart. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Red hair." He'd never seen hair that deeply red, that luxuriously silky. The cat had wanted to play with it while the man had wanted to do much, much more intimate things.</i>
</b><br /><br />Moreover, Faith needs to prove her trustworthiness to the pack and Vaughn needs to help her identify the person that haunts her dreams and her psychological stability.<br /><br />At the same time the Psy Council needs a replacement for the murderer and sadist Santano Enrique who was eliminated and apparently Faith is a suitable candidate. <br />Will she choose Vaughn and an unknown future or her career and a stable future?<br /><br />I am totally hooked on this series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13075892901177098221" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1581216383" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1581216383" />
    <a title="Kate" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13603287-kate"><img alt="Kate" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531664914p2/13603287.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1581216383?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kate" href="/user/show/13603287-kate">Kate</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11683498-visions-of-heat">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=gives-me-the-tingles">gives-me-the-tingles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=guys-be-a-steaming">guys-be-a-steaming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=broody-alphas">broody-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=bliming-hilarious">bliming-hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=pnr-uf-fantasy-steampunk">pnr-uf-fantasy-steampunk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=wounded-warriors">wounded-warriors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13603287-kate?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1581216383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14478038386276222243">Bookwise at the moment is slim pickings so I've decided to do some rereads.<br/><br/>First read 27/03/2018 - 28/03/2016 - 5 ★<br/>Currently rereading 26/06/2018 - 27/06/2018 nothing has changed still 5 ★<br/>3rd reread - 4th May 2020.<br/><br/><b>I’m actually quite annoyed with myself that I didn’t start this series sooner. I’ve been missing out big time and I’m really regretting it. ⇦ Still true. <br/><br/>Personally I think that the first books cannot be read as standalones as this is a build up to an extraordinary world and that it is</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14478038386276222243" style="display:none">Bookwise at the moment is slim pickings so I've decided to do some rereads.<br /><br />First read 27/03/2018 - 28/03/2016 - 5 ★<br />Currently rereading 26/06/2018 - 27/06/2018 nothing has changed still 5 ★<br />3rd reread - 4th May 2020.<br /><br /><b>I’m actually quite annoyed with myself that I didn’t start this series sooner. I’ve been missing out big time and I’m really regretting it. ⇦ Still true. <br /><br />Personally I think that the first books cannot be read as standalones as this is a build up to an extraordinary world and that it is important to start from the beginning. You have to be prepared to be in it for the long haul. It makes complex and there are layers upon layers of emotions here. <br /><br />5 blood for blood, flesh for flesh, life for life Stars. <br /><br /><u>The Characters &amp; Chemistry.</u><br /><br />Faith NightStar is one of the most talented F-Psy out there she has a strong foresight that has only ever been cultivated for business predictions but as with Sascha things are changing with her Psy state. <br /><br />As there are some dangers of having foresight going clinical insane is one of them, F-Psy’s are kept isolated and there health is monitored for their own good, of course. It doesn’t matter that Faith makes billions. She is strongly tied to the silence that is until she starts seeing things that don’t fit the norm. She looks for the one person that won’t betray her to the council and that is Sascha Duncan. <br /><br />Vaughn D’Angelo is a jaguar shifter, he is wilder than the others in the leopard pack. His childhood and the loss of his sister had a great impact on his jaguar and him as a human. He is a sentinel for DarkRiver and is fascinated by the house in the woods that houses a single Psy. He can’t leave it alone until he sees a Psy trying to escape and follows Faith. <br /><br />Once again this is an exceptional read, with a complex world that gives you enough information to be sucked in but without being overwhelmed. <br /><br />Faith has great character development and she goes from someone not being able to be touched at all to the person that she is meant to be. Vaughn &amp; Faith’s interactions are different to Sacha &amp; Lucas. Although there is great humour and banter between the two it just feels different. <br /><br />“Sounds like fear to me,” Vaughn said. “I’m Psy I don’t feel fear.” His focus on her was so intense, she felt stripped bare. “Then what would you call it?” “A physiological reaction to unknown stress factors.<br /><br />Their affection for one another was palpable and it grew even more with each encounter that they had. Vaughn liked to push Faith’s boundaries. <br /><br />“I wasn’t thinking about stroking you.” She preceded him down the hallway. “I was imagining your fur.” Heat at her back and a rough whisper against her ear. “You let me stroke you and I’ll let you stroke me- I have a thing about your skin”<br /><br />There are so many twists and turns of the NetMind and the turmoil on the PsyNet and that the Psy are slowly losing control to the repression and the eradication of emotions. The development of the NetMind and how they interacted was amazing, I really liked that scenario and NS fully develops this throughout the other books. <br /><br />Ms. Singh manages to make the relationship between Faith &amp; Vaughn completely unique. Sometimes authors have a cookie cutter heroine that they stick to but I like the fact that it isn’t the case here. <br /><br />I loved every single moment of this book and for the fact that I couldn’t sleep last night I got to read more of it. ⇦ So very true. <br /><br />I have my doubts about Judd Lauren in the next book but I will give him a chance. I also get to see more of Hawke and the SnowDancers. I don#t have any doubts anymore as I love Judd. He will be the next reread.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14478038386276222243" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/75717048?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2014-reads">2014-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer75717048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7108164259174771492"><br/><b>4 "love the story" stars!</b><br/><br/><i>This review includes my thoughts on the audio version.</i><br/><br/>This world that Nalini Singh has created is amazing. Absolutely enthralling! I love the way the stories unfold, the trials, the triumphs... it's a brilliant world, overall.<br/><br/>This particular story was a bit slow to start, and I had some problems getting into it. But once things started rolling, I was hooked and couldn't get through it fast enough.<br/><br/>I wasn't as impressed with Angela Dawe's narration this time. She does a gr</span>
  <span id="freeText7108164259174771492" style="display:none"><br /><b>4 "love the story" stars!</b><br /><br /><i>This review includes my thoughts on the audio version.</i><br /><br />This world that Nalini Singh has created is amazing. Absolutely enthralling! I love the way the stories unfold, the trials, the triumphs... it's a brilliant world, overall.<br /><br />This particular story was a bit slow to start, and I had some problems getting into it. But once things started rolling, I was hooked and couldn't get through it fast enough.<br /><br />I wasn't as impressed with Angela Dawe's narration this time. She does a great job with the Psy... their lack of emotion, the awe in their voices as they begin to see the world the way it really is... she's great with them, but I'm having problems with her portrayal of the Changelings.<br /><br />I highly recommend this series to fans who like steam with their Sci-Fi and Urban Fantasy.<br /><br /><b>Breaking it down:</b><br /><br />Overall Psy-Changeling World: 5 stars<br />This particular storyline: 4 stars<br />Narration: 3 stars <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7108164259174771492" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_145022143" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/145022143" />
    <a title="Leah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3050338-leah"><img alt="Leah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474253068p2/3050338.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/145022143?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leah" href="/user/show/3050338-leah">Leah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Leah by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4208075-karen-divhine">Karen ~ Divhine</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=adult-lit">adult-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer145022143" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14411526701849612134">Visions of Heat is the second book in Nalini Singh's Psy/Changeling series and yet another great installment. Like I said in my review of Slave to Sensation, I did not expect to like this series. As a matter of fact, I figured that I would read the first one and have no desire to continue the series. Boy was I ever wrong. I'm sitting here at 1:52 A.M. wishing that I had the third book so I could start it right away tomorrow. Alas, it is not to be. But damn, I really need to get out and buy these</span>
  <span id="freeText14411526701849612134" style="display:none">Visions of Heat is the second book in Nalini Singh's Psy/Changeling series and yet another great installment. Like I said in my review of Slave to Sensation, I did not expect to like this series. As a matter of fact, I figured that I would read the first one and have no desire to continue the series. Boy was I ever wrong. I'm sitting here at 1:52 A.M. wishing that I had the third book so I could start it right away tomorrow. Alas, it is not to be. But damn, I really need to get out and buy these books!<br /><br />I loved the way that Singh continued to built the world she created for this series. And I have to say, I don't even really feel like it's in the future. You know how with some books you can tell from the technology, people, whatever that you are in a completely different time? Not so with this series. It actually came as a bit of a shock when I was reading Slave to Sensation reviews and someone mentioned that the series takes place in 2079. I'd say that's a sign of great writing when something so out of the ordinary can feel so natural.<br /><br />Politics, particularly those of the Psy, played a major role in Visions of Heat, much more than it did in Slave to Sensation, and while I generally do not enjoy reading anything that is strongly based in politics, I found that I actually really enjoyed those aspects. I think, though, that's because it was so critical, so pivotal in Faith's life that it would have felt...empty if those political aspects had been absent, whether they be entirely absent or just there to a lesser extent. I also liked the political aspect because it made Faith's struggle and decision that much more realistic to me because, while I was frustrated that she didn't immediately decide to go off with Vaughn, I could understand: How do you choose to leave everything you've ever known behind, even if it's not what it's always appeared to be, for a world, life, and culture that you've never even experienced? Not an easy choice and one that I liked to see Faith struggle with because, while I like to think it would be easy to follow the love of my life into the unknown, I know that is entirely unrealistic.<br /><br />Speaking of Faith and Vaughn, I continued to like the characters. Obviously most of them are the same people from the previous book, but I liked getting to see more of them. Sascha and Lucas had a clear presence in the book but I loved the glimpses into Dorian and Clay, and I even liked seeing a little more of Judd, even though I'm not quite sure just how I feel about him yet. And when it came to the main characters? I loved them too. Faith was a brilliant character and I enjoyed reading about her struggles to find her sister's murderer, to find herself and realize how strong she really is. All in all, though, I still preferred Sascha, but Faith was an intriguing character to follow throughout the book. Now, Vaughn, I definitely love him more than Lucas. Dorian still remains my favorite male thus far, but I couldn't help but utterly adore Vaughn. He's much more animalistic than the other men so he always had more of a wild, feral edge to him than anyone else and that appealed to me more than Lucas ever did. Vaughn was exceptionally possessive and protective and, really, how could you not love the guy? Like with the world-building, I love how Singh continues to make me love her characters by showing me different facets of them all the time.<br /><br />I have to say again how glad I am that I jumped on this bandwagon. I can't believe I've been so resistant for so long. This series is quickly becoming a favorite and I feel the distinct urge to run out to the store and buy all the books. Too bad it's 2:00 in the morning and I don't have the money for it. Oh well, a girl can dream, right?</span>
  <a data-text-id="14411526701849612134" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet"><img alt="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387046887p2/13567836.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2577218514?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11683498-visions-of-heat">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=paranomal-general">paranomal-general</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=2-stars">2-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-romance">pn-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=insta-love-lust-connection">insta-love-lust-connection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet?shelf=pn-shapeshifters">pn-shapeshifters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2577218514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6931214762146661233"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*I didn't like it*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/>The second book in the series centers around the F-Psy, - highly sought after ability to predict the future - <b>Faith ‘Red’ NightStar</b> (24) and Changeling jaguar <b>Vaughn D'Angelo</b>. We met Vaughn in book one were we see him as one of <b>Lucas Hunter</b>'s sentinels and is Lucas’s closest friend. Vaughn was far more animal than most predatory changelings, had had to become so to survive. Faith of the PsyClan NightStar was considered the most powerful F-Psy of her generation; </span>
  <span id="freeText6931214762146661233" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*I didn't like it*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br />The second book in the series centers around the F-Psy, - highly sought after ability to predict the future - <b>Faith ‘Red’ NightStar</b> (24) and Changeling jaguar <b>Vaughn D'Angelo</b>. We met Vaughn in book one were we see him as one of <b>Lucas Hunter</b>'s sentinels and is Lucas’s closest friend. Vaughn was far more animal than most predatory changelings, had had to become so to survive. Faith of the PsyClan NightStar was considered the most powerful F-Psy of her generation; she’d already made more money than most Psy did in their entire lifetimes. But then again, she’d been working since she was three years old. Faith believes she's going mad and decides she needs <b>Sascha Duncan</b>. Vaughn is immediately fascinated by the red head and quickly decides he isn't going to let her walk away. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Faith NightStar of the PsyClan NightStar was aware she was considered the most powerful F-Psy of her generation. At only twenty-four years of age, she’d already made more money than most Psy did in their entire lifetimes. But then again, she’d been working since she was three years old, since she’d found her voice. It had taken her longer than most children, but that was to be expected—she was a cardinal F-Psy of extraordinary ability.<br />It would have surprised no one if she’d never spoken.<br />That was why the F-Psy belonged to PsyClans, which took care of everything the foreseers couldn’t, from investing their millions to checking their medical status to ensuring they didn’t starve. The F-Psy weren’t very good at practical things like that. They forgot. Even after more than a century of forecasting business trends rather than murders and accidents, disasters and wars, they forgot.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Overall, I was bored. It wasn't long into the book I started skimming. <b>The book gave of the feeling of insta-love</b> as the timeline was just under few weeks; two are most. I also didn't connect with either character, they let me quite indifferent and uncaring. Worst of all, it made me decide I didn't want to continue the rest of the series. The book felt like a repeat with the same female character, just different name. However, <b>I didn't like Faith all that much for some reason</b>, she was just there. Taking up space and all that. Vaughn couldn't compare to Lucas at all, and I couldn't find it in me to feel anything more than 'he's alright'.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Lucas stroked his fingers over his mate’s cheek and Vaughn wanted to do the same with Faith. Delicate, icy, she was hardly the type of woman who usually attracted him, but there was something fascinating about her, something compelling.<br />“How old were you when they started training you?” he asked his Psy. He’d found her first. Therefore, she was his. It was the cat talking and Vaughn didn’t feel like arguing.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br />↦ <b>Xi Yun</b>, the head M-Psy.<br />↦ <b>Anthony Kyriakus NightStar</b>, Faith's father and the head of her family. Until she’d officially reached adulthood at twenty, he’d shared custody of her with <b>Zanna Liskowski</b>, with whom he’d formed a fertilization contract twenty-five years ago. At three years after birth, she’d been removed from their care, with their full cooperation, and placed in a controlled environment where her ability could be fully trained and utilized.<br />↦ <b>Sascha Duncan</b>, an E-Psy—an empath, able to sense and heal the most damaging of emotional wounds. She's <b>Lucas Hunter</b>'s mate. Lucas is Vaughn pack alpha.<br />↦ <b>Marine</b>, Faith's younger sister, a sister she’d never really known, but had kept an eye on from afar. A cardinal telepath, Marine had already climbed high in the family’s interests. Marine was dead and Faith had foreseen her murder without knowing she had seen it. The killer isn't finished killing.<br />↦ <b>Kaleb Krychek</b> (26), a cardinal Tk and part of the Council ranks, his control over his telekenetic abilities is reputed to be superb. He's a candidate for replacement for Councilor <b>Santano Enrique</b>, a killer who died in book one.<br />↦ <b>Sienna Lauren</b>, the Psys believe she dead; she showed great potential. Councilor member <b>Ming LeBon</b> had his eye on her as a possible protégée. Which could only mean that Sienna Lauren had been born with the mental combat abilities that made Ming so deadly. <br />↦ <b>Gia Khan</b>, a M-Psy and candidate to be one the council. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Human women have been slapping men for being bastards for centuries. You were doing what comes naturally.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br /><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance<br /><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Two. <br /><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Favorite character?</b> - Lucas Hunter.<br /><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br /><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Just the first one.<br /><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br /><b>Rating</b> - 2 stars.</span>

    <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans"><img alt="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587115780p2/7298986.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)" href="/user/show/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans">✘✘ Sarah ✘✘ (former Nefarious Breeder of Murderous Crustaceans)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9308838-visions-of-heat">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7298986-sarah-former-nefarious-breeder-of-murderous-crustaceans?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1122941072" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10964526680975162379"><b>2.5 meh stars + 0.5 stars for the world building.</b> <br/><br/><b>What went wrong here? I don't really know.</b> It just feels like I've just read a poor version of <b>Slave to Sensation</b>, with more romance and less suspense/action. <br/><br/><b>The world building is still great</b> but I expected Singh to dig a bit deeper here. Granted, the <b>NetMind/DarkMind</b> thing is pretty cool and we get to learn a bit more about the <b>Silence Protocol</b> but that's as far as Singh goes in terms of world expansion which is <b>a bit disappointing.</b> There is ta</span>
  <span id="freeText10964526680975162379" style="display:none"><b>2.5 meh stars + 0.5 stars for the world building.</b> <br /><br /><b>What went wrong here? I don't really know.</b> It just feels like I've just read a poor version of <b>Slave to Sensation</b>, with more romance and less suspense/action. <br /><br /><b>The world building is still great</b> but I expected Singh to dig a bit deeper here. Granted, the <b>NetMind/DarkMind</b> thing is pretty cool and we get to learn a bit more about the <b>Silence Protocol</b> but that's as far as Singh goes in terms of world expansion which is <b>a bit disappointing.</b> There is talk of revolution within the Psy-Net though so <b>I still have high hopes for the rest of the series.</b><br /><br /><b>I have to admit that I was a bit taken aback</b> when I first started reading this book because I thought it was going to be about Sascha &amp; Lucas. I never expected it to be about different characters. Is this the way PNR series work? <b>Once I got past the initial surprise</b> I was happy to read about new characters but the problem here is that they aren't as strong as in the previous book. Worse, <b>I had a hard time connecting with them.</b> Vaughn is too much the typical dark/brooding/loner alpha and <b>Faith is pretty uninteresting.</b> Wait, let's not be too harsh here, there is something interesting about Faith: <b>her father.</b> I'm really curious about him and I can't wait to see what Singh does with his characters. <br /><br /><b>The sexual chemistry between Vaughn &amp; Faith isn't that great</b> and the sex scenes themselves were disappointing and not as well written as the ones between Sascha &amp; Lucas. <b>So no, Visions of Heat didn't have me throwing my underwear across the room.</b> Too bad, I was more than willing to.<br /><br /><b>Although this was a disappointing read</b> I still want to continue with this series. I love the world building too much to give up now and I'm told <b>Caressed by Iced</b> is one of the best instalments in the series. I didn't really like what I saw of Judd here but <b>I can't wait to see how this particular iceman thaws *rubs hands in anticipation*</b></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer516184461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11511503192472817582"><br/><b>4 1/2 Stars for the Voracious Vaughn!</b> Unbelievably sensual, passionate, irrefutable character chemistry, yet the story isn’t overloaded with descriptive sexual details. The writing is near orgasmic and Nalini Singh knows how to make her readers feel as much as the characters in her books! I found myself reading with my mouth slightly parted, and I might have even been panting!! How embarrassing!! <br/><br/>Not quite as captivating as the first book, bogged down in a little too much detail, where the overa</span>
  <span id="freeText11511503192472817582" style="display:none"><br /><b>4 1/2 Stars for the Voracious Vaughn!</b> Unbelievably sensual, passionate, irrefutable character chemistry, yet the story isn’t overloaded with descriptive sexual details. The writing is near orgasmic and Nalini Singh knows how to make her readers feel as much as the characters in her books! I found myself reading with my mouth slightly parted, and I might have even been panting!! How embarrassing!! <br /><br />Not quite as captivating as the first book, bogged down in a little too much detail, where the overall plot and villain where concerned. I’m not sure if I grasped all that happened. I had the audio and eBook at my disposal, and found myself bouncing between the two to get a handle on the storyline, at times I felt I needed the written word to clarify what I was hearing and vice versa, it was somewhat complicated. <b>However…</b>this is a series that is definitely worth sticking with. There are just too many intriguing characters that need my attention. Nalini Singh has drawn me into a world where passion rules, and there are those willing to risk everything for the chance to feel!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11511503192472817582" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3191326706" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3191326706?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3191326706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer88088901707047824"><b>The perfect amount of <i>Heat</i>...</b><br/><br/><i>Visions of Heat</i> is a very well written story and <i>Nalini Singh</i> manages to bring the <i>Psy-Changeling</i> world and characters to life for me. The storyline kept me interested from start to finish and I never found myself bored or struggling to go on. I was drawn to the Changelings as being the right and good side, while also finding parts of the Psy appealing even though they are portrayed as the wrong side. I liked the touchy-feely part of being pack but would hate being t</span>
  <span id="freeText88088901707047824" style="display:none"><b>The perfect amount of <i>Heat</i>...</b><br><br><i>Visions of Heat</i> is a very well written story and <i>Nalini Singh</i> manages to bring the <i>Psy-Changeling</i> world and characters to life for me. The storyline kept me interested from start to finish and I never found myself bored or struggling to go on. I was drawn to the Changelings as being the right and good side, while also finding parts of the Psy appealing even though they are portrayed as the wrong side. I liked the touchy-feely part of being pack but would hate being touched all the time. I liked the idea of not being controlled by my emotions but hate the idea of not feeling...anything.<br><br>I loved Faith and Vaughn together and enjoyed their journey to happiness. It was appealing that their love story was not rushed and it wasn't 'insta-mating-bond' like a lot of other similar stories. I liked that while Vaughn was intensely attracted to Faith, he was so patient with her and knew that her sensitivity to touch was not something to be pushed. The <i>Heat</i> level was perfect. There was enough <i>Heat</i> to get my heart pumping without being OTT or too much. It was sexy, sensual and passionate. <br><br>This series is quickly becoming a favourite and I will definitely be going on to see the Council crumble and the Changelings take over the world... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1548709401i/26982519.jpg" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer40406893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11939776108074779674">5 stars – Paranormal Romance <br/><br/><b>Visions of Heat</b> is a fantastic second book that goes further into the escalating conflict between the emotionless, cold, psychically powerful Psy race and the Changelings (shifters that are both human and animal) in the year 2079.<br/><br/>Faith Nightstar is a powerful F-Psy, a foreseer, who has been completely isolated due to the dangerous power and strain of her potent psychic ability and used for the monetary gain of the Psy-Council. But lately she’s been tormented by distu</span>
  <span id="freeText11939776108074779674" style="display:none">5 stars – Paranormal Romance <br /><br /><b>Visions of Heat</b> is a fantastic second book that goes further into the escalating conflict between the emotionless, cold, psychically powerful Psy race and the Changelings (shifters that are both human and animal) in the year 2079.<br /><br />Faith Nightstar is a powerful F-Psy, a foreseer, who has been completely isolated due to the dangerous power and strain of her potent psychic ability and used for the monetary gain of the Psy-Council. But lately she’s been tormented by disturbing and violent visions of the future, and escapes to seek help from Sascha, a Psy defector, and the DarkRiver leopard pack. Changeling Vaughn D’Angelo is the sole jaguar among the leopard pack and the most volatile. Faith stirs the inner cravings and hungers of his beast that he’s long denied, and Vaughn becomes determined to shatter her fragile wall of Silence and claim her as his mate. Their relationship threatens to further damage the tentative co-existence between the Psy-Changelings.<br /><br />Vaughn is a dominant, forceful, and arrogant hero who’s almost more jaguar than man, which is sexy-as-all-get-out to me, and his passion and love for Faith is strong. Their romance is sweet and sexy, and there are some steamy hot love scenes. It’s a great second installment in an original, amazing paranormal series that truly stands out in the genre. 5 stars!<br /></span>

<div id="review_124090391" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124090391" />
    <a title=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida"><img alt=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1295034921p2/1453659.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/124090391?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*" href="/user/show/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida"> Lady Jayne *~*The Beach Bandida*~*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=owned-read">owned-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=author-nalini-singh">author-nalini-singh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1453659-lady-jayne-the-beach-bandida?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer124090391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11156538963826859057"><p><i>Also reviewed at: <a href='http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com/2011/08/review-visions-of-heat-2-psychangeling.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a></i><br/><br/><b>4.5 Stars? Aaahhh... Make it 5!</b> ^_^ <b><blockquote>
<i>“Tell a child something often enough and she starts to believe it.”</i> ~ Sascha to Faith</blockquote></b>*sigh* I LOVED this book even more the second time around!! <br/><br/>While my re-read of <b><i>Slave to Sensation</i></b> had me dreaming (again!) about being enslaved by the delicious Lucas Hunter *grins*... it more seriously had me contemplating the concept of a “society without emotion” that is the Psy. In my re-read of <i><b>Visions of Heat</b></i>, the theme that be</p></span>
  <span id="freeText11156538963826859057" style="display:none"><p><i>Also reviewed at: <a href="http://ladyjaynesreadingden.blogspot.com/2011/08/review-visions-of-heat-2-psychangeling.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Jayne's Reading Den</a></i><br><br><b>4.5 Stars? Aaahhh... Make it 5!</b> ^_^ <b><blockquote>
<i>“Tell a child something often enough and she starts to believe it.”</i> ~ Sascha to Faith</blockquote></b>*sigh* I LOVED this book even more the second time around!! <br><br>While my re-read of <b><i>Slave to Sensation</i></b> had me dreaming (again!) about being enslaved by the delicious Lucas Hunter *grins*... it more seriously had me contemplating the concept of a “society without emotion” that is the Psy. In my re-read of <i><b>Visions of Heat</b></i>, the theme that became the focus of my reflections - which was also a prevalent theme in the first book - was that of having the strength to free one’s “self” from the "prison" imposed by others, and of seeing things we were blind to before.<br><br>Faith Nighstar, of the PsyClan NightStar, is a powerful “F-Psy” – a cardinal Psy with the ability of foresight. Since the age of 3, she has been isolated from society and trained to give business forecasts, worth billions. She has also been told that the F-Psy are particularly susceptible to madness. That for her own protection, she must be constantly monitored and undergo medical tests, regularly.<br><br>Now, at the age of 24, Faith is starting to have some very dark dreams, malevolent visions of blood and murder. She thinks - not <i>“fears”</i>, as the Psy are not supposed to fear - that insanity is looming. In an effort to get more information, without alerting her keepers of her degeneration, Faith decides to seek out Sascha Duncan, a renegade Psy who is now part of the DarkRiver changeling leopard pack.<br><br>Vaughn D’Angelo, a jaguar adopted into the leopard pack through a tragic event, whose beast prowls closer to the surface than other changelings, is a sentinel of DarkRiver. He has recently become very curious about an isolated compound, in which appears to live a Psy. The Psy usually choose to live in skyscrapers. <br><br>When Faith escapes the compound to seek out Sascha, it is Vaughn who finds her in DarkRiver territory. Vaughn’s cat side is immediately instinctually drawn to Faith and can’t stop teasing and bombarding her senses with his touch. This puzzles Vaughn, the man, as he does not believe in the concept of “mating”, not wanting to ever need anyone or have someone need him. <br><br>I was drawn into Vaughn and Faith’s story: Vaughn, as he works though his conflicted feelings towards Faith; as he sees her as not just a cold Psy, but a fascinating woman he wants to tease and protect, and as he realises that while he has "mated" with Faith, she can refuse that mating bond. Faith, as she tries to buckle “Silence”, to find pleasure in Vaughn’s touch, and to allow herself to feel. I felt for the losses they had both suffered – Vaughn’s story, particularly, broke my heart. I admired Faith as she fought not to fall into the madness of her dark visions; as she started to “see” that the things she has been told all her life were lies. How does Faith break through the walls that isolate and imprison her, when they are so much a part of “her”? <br><br>I appreciated the intriguing political aspects that Nalini Singh included in this book - and also in the first - through the machinations of the Psy Council. <br><br>Through my re-read, I found the initially bewildering, complex concept of the PsyNet easier to process.<br><br>There were a few loose threads at the end of this book, which I’m expecting will be answered later in the series…at least, I hope so!<br><br>P.S. I DO NOT like the cover of this book and the guy looks nothing like how Vaughn is described! In fact, a lot of the covers in this amazing series by Nalini Singh just don't do it justice, in my humble opinion.<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <i>“Faith looked up. And up. As she’d guessed from the feel of him at her back, the jaguar was tall in human form. His hair was a thick amber-gold, long enough to brush his shoulders, and his eyes ... they were an odd almost-gold, the eyes of a cat made human. There was nothing soft about him, nothing tame. Yet she, a woman who'd never before understood the concept, found him beautiful. It was an inexplicable reaction, one her brain couldn't accept, going as it did against every rule of Silence.”</i>
</blockquote> <br><i>
  <b>Vaughn is prrrimally sexxxy…</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379763454i/219671.jpg" width="270" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>
  <b>His jaguar is strong within him…</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696562.png" width="350" height="230" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>
  <b>Vaughn needs to live in the wilds of nature….</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696563.jpg" width="320" height="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>
  <b>Faith has only known a sterile Psy environment…</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696564.jpg" width="300" height="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Now Faith’s night-sky eyes have opened…</b>
</i> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380340019i/696565.jpg" width="230" height="330" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>And her senses explode under Vaughn’s heated touch - RAWR!!! Can Vaughn help Faith break free of her prison?</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379763454i/219670.jpg" width="250" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><b>Psy/Changeling Series Reading Order:</b><br><br>1. Slave to Sensation - (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/123758242" rel="nofollow noopener">Review here</a>)<br>1.5 "The Cannibal Princess" - Free short story:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.php#princess">http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.p...</a> - (<a>Review here</a>)<br>2. Visions of Heat<br>3. Caressed By Ice - To be reviewed.<br>4. Mine to Possess - (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/124090396" rel="nofollow noopener">Review here</a>) <br>5. Hostage to Pleasure - To be reviewed.<br>5.5 "A Gift for Kit" - Free short story: <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.php#gift">http://www.nalinisingh.com/freebies.p...</a><br>6. Branded By Fire<br>7. Blaze of Memory<br>8. Bonds of Justice <br>9. Play of Passion<br>10. Kiss of Snow<br><br>And there are also stand-alone novellas:<br>1. "Beat of Temptation" in An Enchanted Season<br>2. "Stroke of Enticement" in The Magical Christmas Cat<br>3. "Whisper of Sin" in Burning Up<br><br>But if you wish to read in strict chronological order, see Nalini Singh's website (link to the page here): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.nalinisingh.com/psybehind.php">http://www.nalinisingh.com/psybehind.php</a><br><br><br><i>COPYRIGHT DISCLAIMER: I do not hold the copyright to any of the images used in this review. They are posted to add visuals to the review and for fun. If any of these images are yours and you would like me to remove them, please let me know, and I will do so as soon as possible. <div id="review_582976287" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/582976287" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/582976287?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8255988-visions-of-heat">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=aoc">aoc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=review-books-done">review-books-done</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2013-read">2013-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2019-read">2019-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582976287" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16744099334148473504">To be honest, this, <em>Visions of Heat</em>, has always been one of my least favorite books in this series - I'm not sure how much that's actually saying, considering most of these books rate beyond my scale of awesomeness, but there are issues (and I look over my previous notes after this re-read, it didn't always hit me as strongly as it did this time, but the issues were always there for me).<br/><br/>My number one biggest issue? Vaughn. Especially in the first 35% or so of the book. He's a pushy asshole. Ther</span>
  <span id="freeText16744099334148473504" style="display:none">To be honest, this, <em>Visions of Heat</em>, has always been one of my least favorite books in this series - I'm not sure how much that's actually saying, considering most of these books rate beyond my scale of awesomeness, but there are issues (and I look over my previous notes after this re-read, it didn't always hit me as strongly as it did this time, but the issues were always there for me).<br /><br />My number one biggest issue? Vaughn. Especially in the first 35% or so of the book. He's a pushy asshole. There's a quote in the book that I think encapsulates my problems with him, especially in the beginning (and I'll get into why it's not as bad later in the book).<br /><blockquote>
  <strong><em>Careful, Faith.</em> <em>He won't stop when you tell him to.</em></strong>
</blockquote><br />Now, this is one sentence out of the entire book, but it's where my problem lies. Some background: Faith, a cardinal F-Psy ('F' for Foresight) has been isolated from the time she was three, THREE, years old. She's had close to no physical contact (other than the occasional medical exam or treatment), and she's been conditioned to believe that interacting with people, or touch, could set her off into a cascade that will leave her insane. Clinically insane. Showing more strength than even she knows she has, she walks into DarkRiver territory, looking for Sascha and help, and runs into Vaughn.<br /><br />He doesn't know her. He doesn't trust her. I get all that. What I don't get, and what I'm not okay with, is him using his body - his sexuality - to make her uncomfortable. I'm not okay with the fact that he uses touch, and his judgment on what's enough or too much, against her express wishes. No Means No. Also, Silence Does Not Mean Yes. Only Yes Means Yes. These are not catch-phrases. They need to become reality and truth and the only acceptable idea.<br /><br />Vaughn argues that he's trying to make her stronger, to "sensitize" her to the world. It doesn't matter that he actually is making her stronger. It doesn't matter that Silence is wrong. It doesn't matter that she'll be better off once she's able to accept feelings and emotions. Within a couple of hours of meeting her, HE is making decisions that could affect, not only her welfare, but her physical and mental health. What matters is that though she finally does concede to *some* touch, he <em>still</em> doesn't stop when she says<strong> enough</strong>.<br /><br />It does matter that when he starts to lose control, and become more <em>cat</em>, that she puts aside her own welfare and concern to ensure that he's taken care of. To touch him as <strong>he </strong>needs. Never mind her needs. Never mind the fact that the pain is so intense - and she never lets him see it - that it makes her lose consciousness.<br /><br />None of this is okay. I know that in my thoughts on this book before, I've articulated that it's not one of my favorites, that it's a weaker entry in the series, and that Vaughn's pushiness irritated me. It went beyond that this time. I get what is trying to be done, and on one level I understand. The Changelings are not human, they never will be. There are different rules at play in this world. But what I've come to realize this read through is that no matter the world, Yes needs to be the only thing that means Yes.<br /><br />Now, that I've gotten that rant out of the way, I'll say that when Faith gets her feet under her it levels out the power disparity that permeates the first third of the novel. She doesn't let him push her around, though - it could be argued that he's getting his way as she's becoming more sensitized to touch and emotion, but I'm not sure I want to go there right now. Faith becomes more than powerful and strong enough to take on Vaughn. But this book suffers because he's too domineering in the beginning and she's made extremely helpless. In the later half of the book, I really begin to love Faith.<br /><br />The story itself is intriguing. There's more revealed about the Psy machinations and reality in particular. But it's the world that really continues to build in this series. We learn more about the Psy, expanding into other groups and affiliations. We learn more about how they respond, how they think, and you begin to see just how huge the problem is that faces everyone in this world. Trust me when I say it's the tip of the iceberg.<br /><br />And trust me when I say that the next book, <em>Caressed by Ice</em>, is absolutely freaking amazing - with none of the problems that this one suffers. In fact, I can't think of another book in the series that suffers from the issues I laid out here.<br /><br />This continues to be a favorite series, and a comfort read for me, but I couldn't ignore the problematic issues in this particular novel anymore.<br /><br />This review is also available at <a href="https://thebookeaters.net/2016/05/07/review-visions-of-heat/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Eaters</a><br /><br /><br />Previous thoughts:<br /><br />I'll admit the first time I read this book I was pretty-damn disappointed. It didn't nearly live up to the love I had for the first book. Vaughn seemed to bond too easily, and the storyline seemed nearly identical to the first book. <br /><br />I've re-read it many times since then. And I have to say that, while it isn't (IMO) as good as Slave to Sensation; it's not as disappointing as I'd originally thought. My expectations were so, so, SO high after StS that nearly anything would have been a let down.<br /><br />The world is still fantastically awesome, and the characters feel <i>real</i>. I mean, obviously they're not real, but they're true to their characters. The romance was sweet (if a lot like the one in StS), and I grew to appreciate Faith a lot more. Vaughn irritated me at times with his pushiness, but overall I still really enjoy this book.<br /><br />Of course, for me, being surrounded by a great first book and the AWESOME third book didn't do Visions of Heat any favors. Because Caressed by Ice is up next and boy, oh boy, is it fantastic.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16744099334148473504" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer5126474303776840282"> ^^ VISIONS OF VAUGHN!^^<br/><br/>If Vaughn was a Tree: I would climb him and make a nest.<br/>A Medium Size Pool: I would do laps all day long.<br/>A Bath Tub: I would soak all day.<br/>If Vaughn was naked, I would be naked too.<br/><br/>I am happy that I enjoyed the second book in the Psy-Changeling series; I was having some doubts after the first one where it took some time to really get into the story. I was in love in love from the moment the very sexy Sentinel named Vaughn mentioned his first words in the book. <br/><br/>Quick rundow</span>
  <span id="freeText5126474303776840282" style="display:none"> ^^ VISIONS OF VAUGHN!^^<br /><br />If Vaughn was a Tree: I would climb him and make a nest.<br />A Medium Size Pool: I would do laps all day long.<br />A Bath Tub: I would soak all day.<br />If Vaughn was naked, I would be naked too.<br /><br />I am happy that I enjoyed the second book in the Psy-Changeling series; I was having some doubts after the first one where it took some time to really get into the story. I was in love in love from the moment the very sexy Sentinel named Vaughn mentioned his first words in the book. <br /><br />Quick rundown, the Psy are a mind race, they feel no emotion and they strive to be perfect or should I say they claim to be perfect. They say cus without feelings there would be no murders, no jealousy and all those other human emotions that causes destruction (Pfffft). The Changelings are shifters, who are all about emotions and getting physical, so lets say these very two races are about to get up close and personal.<br /><br />Faith Nightstar is the money-maker Psy, her visions are worth millions if not billions and they are milking her dry. She also has been having crazy violent dreams, and feels she is slowly going insane. What the Psy race does to defects is to rehabilitate or casually get rid of them. A little adventure to find a Psy woman who left the race behind leads her into Changeling territory, and the arms of a dangerous sentinel.<br /><br />Vaughn aka (I am so sexy I will make your panty drop) is an angry and dark soul. He is deadly and stealth like the Jaguar that he is, and he is dangerous. He lives to protect his alpha and his mate that is until his own mate makes an appearance in the form of Faith (frigid) Nightstar. Vaughn will have to fight to get his woman, and convince her he has the stuff to keep her safe.<br /><br />Well the story pretty much becomes the Faith and Vaughn show, with a murder mystery as the side dish. I am just in love with the Changelings and there touch privileges. Vaughn (sigh) is more animal than man, and that my friends is winner in my book. While reading I was thinking how fast I could lose my clothes if he snuck through my sun roof (really I don’t have a sun roof but am willing to cut a hole in my ceiling). I would go from 0 to 60 in like a second just like a Jaguar (hear me roar/growl).<br /><br />Nalini is building a pretty intriguing world and I am looking forward to all the other Psy-Changeling adventures. Also excited for the Psy man, because guess what dude you can’t hide feelings when you sporting a boner.<br /><br />Vaughn seriously gimme my panties back.<br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1722178737" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32533773-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569168662p2/32533773.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

<div id="review_1623094761" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1623094761" />
    <a title="Anna lost in stories *A*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/46741025-anna-lost-in-stories-a"><img alt="Anna lost in stories *A*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458230118p2/46741025.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1623094761?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna lost in stories *A*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna lost in stories *A*" href="/user/show/46741025-anna-lost-in-stories-a">Anna lost in stories *A*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780575095687" href="/book/show/7179272-visions-of-heat">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46741025-anna-lost-in-stories-a?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/46741025-anna-lost-in-stories-a?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1623094761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16769692500552016743">I continue on with my journey to reread this whole series, and I can already tell you that my opinions and rating will vary much more than when I read them originally years ago… this book being the perfect example :) because after absolutely loving “Slave to sensation”, the first book all about my favourite couple, Sascha and Lucas, this one… was a bit of a disappointment… I was going back and forth about how to rate this particular story and ultimately I landed on 3,5 stars… it may seem harsh, </span>
  <span id="freeText16769692500552016743" style="display:none">I continue on with my journey to reread this whole series, and I can already tell you that my opinions and rating will vary much more than when I read them originally years ago… this book being the perfect example :) because after absolutely loving “Slave to sensation”, the first book all about my favourite couple, Sascha and Lucas, this one… was a bit of a disappointment… I was going back and forth about how to rate this particular story and ultimately I landed on 3,5 stars… it may seem harsh, but make no mistakes, I still quite enjoyed this book… and I absolutely love this world and Nalini’s writing style… but Vaughn, the hero in this one… *sighs* I adore changelings in this world, they are tactile, family oriented and just such a fun to read about… but they can be possessive and confident, often to the point of being arrogant :) and there’s a fine line of how much of that behaviour I can accept… because certain things that came out as playful and teasing when it was Lucas in that first book came out just… too much, when it came to Vaughn… and I do understand that he’s a bit different, and much more intense, even for a changeling, but he was just… too arrogant, too pushy, he wanted way too much way too soon from Faith, basically ignoring what she said… and it kept irritating me to no end… the relationship felt a bit underdeveloped, but I do have to praise Nalini and her mastermind… because she had to have known how the first big story arch would end when she started writing the first book… the foreshadowing and little snippets she put here and there… when you know where it’s all going you can see the bits of foundations she’s woven throughout all of her previous books… and that aspect of the story is amazing ;) looking forward to reading the rest of the series, even though this one wasn’t to my liking :)<br /><br />disclaimer<br />until further notice, I will be adding this little disclaimer at the end of all my reviews… without boring you with unnecessary details I will say this… I’ve been in a writing slump for a while now… it’s happened before, but usually didn’t last very long… it’s connected to a lot of different things in my life, but all those details are personal so I won’t get into them right now… this time unfortunately it’s been already six weeks and it doesn't look like it’s gonna change anytime soon… in all this time I was unable to sit down and write reviews for the books I’ve been reading… and I don’t want to wait any longer, cause I already accumulated quite a few to do… so going forward I will be just writing a very short ones… with maybe an exception here and there if I feel like it ;) I don't want to put pressure on myself to write long and detailed reviews that I used to do for the longest time… instead I will try and add some links to other reviews here on Goodreads if I see ones that I feel share my thoughts and opinions on the stories I read… in the meantime I wish you all happy reading :)<br /><br />XOXO<br /><br />A</span>
  <a data-text-id="16769692500552016743" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
